verses whichare not found in Pāli  The general purport is something like this Iexpound the meaning of Vinaya ‘so that the good law may longremain in the world and all beings fully enjoy its benefit By the meritof this I desire to dispel all evils hatantarāyo  If  one wishes tokeep the precept sīla one should keep it until one is freed from allsufferings As to vv and  only the first half of  and the
